51|41|No mu nkuru y’aba Adi (harimo isomo), ubwo twabohererezaga umuyaga ugumbahaye (udafite icyiza na kimwe, usenya nta cyo usize)
51|42|Nta cyo wasigaga mu byo wahuraga na byo utakigize umuyonga
51|43|No mu nkuru y’aba Thamudu (harimo isomo) ubwo babwirwaga bati “Nimwishimishe by’igihe gito.”
51|44|Ariko bigometse ku itegeko rya Nyagasani wabo, maze bakubitwa n’ikibatsi cy’umuriro w’inkuba bareba
51|45|Ntibashoboraga guhaguruka (ngo bahunge) cyangwa ngo bitabare
51|46|N’abantu ba Nuhu (ni uko twabagenje) mbere. Mu by’ukuri bari abantu b’ibyigomeke
51|47|Kandi ikirere twacyubakanye imbaraga, kandi mu by’ukuri nitwe tucyagura
51|48|N’isi twarayishashe; kandi ni twe dusasa neza
51|49|No muri buri kintu twaremyemo amoko abiri (ikigabo n’ikigore, iburyo n’ibumoso, hasi no hejuru,…) kugira ngo mwibuke (ubushobozi bwa Allah)
51|50|Bityo, nimuhungire kwa Allah. Mu by’ukuri njye (Muhamadi) ndi umuburizi wanyu ugaragara umuturutseho
51|51|Kandi ntimuzabangikanye Allah n’ikigirwamana icyo ari cyo cyose. Mu by’ukuri njye (Muhamadi) ndi umuburizi wanyu ugaragara umuturutseho
51|52|Ni nk’uko, nta ntumwa n’imwe yageze ku babayeho mbere yabo ngo babure kuvuga bati “Ni umurozi cyangwa umusazi!”
51|53|Ese (imvugo nk’izi) barazihererekanyaga? (Oya, si uko bimeze), ahubwo bose bari abantu barengera (imbibi za Allah)
51|54|Bityo (yewe Muhamadi) birengagize kandi ntuzabigayirwa (kuko wamaze gusohoza ubutumwa)
51|55|Unibutse kuko mu by’ukuri urwibutso rugirira akamaro abemeramana
51|56|Kandi nta kindi naremeye amajini n’abantu bitari ukugira ngo bangaragire
51|57|Simbakeneyeho amafunguro, ndetse nta n’ubwo mbakeneyeho ko bangaburira
51|58|Mu by’ukuri Allah ni We Utanga amafunguro, Nyirimbaraga, Ukomeye bihebuje
51|59|Kandi rwose abakora ibibi bazagira umugabane (w’ibihano) umeze nk’umugabane wa bagenzi babo (abababanjirije); bityo, bareke kunsaba kwihutisha (kubahana)
51|60|Ibihano bikomeye bizaba kuri ba bandi bahakanye bitewe n’umunsi basezeranyijwe
52|1|Ndahiye Umusozi wa Twuur
52|2|N’igitabo cyanditse (Qur’an)
52|3|Ku mpapuro zikozwe mu ruhu (rusukuye) ruramburwa (kugira ngo gisomwe)
52|4|N’ingoro (yo mu ijuru) ihora isurwa (n’abamalayika)
52|5|N’igisenge gihanitse (ikirere)
52|6|N’inyanja zibirinduye (ku munsi w’imperuka)
52|7|Mu by’ukuri ibihano bya Nyagasani wawe bizabaho nta kabuza
52|8|Ntagishobora kuzabikumira
52|9|Umunsi ikirere kizatigita umutingito (ukomeye)
52|10|N’imisozi ikagenda (nk’uko ibicu bigenda)
52|11|Kuri uwo munsi ibihano bikomeye bizaba ku bahinyuye (ukuri)
52|12|Ba bandi bahugira mu kwishimisha mu biganiro byuzuye ibinyoma, bidafite akamaro
52|13|Umunsi bazasunikirwa mu muriro wa Jahanamu ku ngufu
52|14|(Bazabwirwa bati) “Uyu ni wo muriro mwajyaga muhinyura.”
52|15|Ese ibi (bihano mubona) ni uburozi cyangwa ntimubona
52|16|Ngaho nimuhiremo, kandi mwabyihanganira cyangwa mutabyihanganira, byose ni kimwe kuri mwe. Mu by’ukuri (ibyo muri kubona) ni ibihembo by’ibyo mwakoraga
52|17|Mu by’ukuri abagandukira (Allah) bazaba bari mu busitani n’inema (bihoraho)
52|18|Binezeza mu byo Nyagasani wabo yabahaye, ndetse no kuba Nyagasani wabo yabarinze ibihano by’umuriro
52|19|(Bazabwirwa bati) “Nimurye munanywe kandi mugubwe neza kubera ibyo mwajyaga mukora.”
52|20|Bazaba begamye ku bitanda bitondetse ku murongo. Tuzanabashyingira Huur ul-a’in (abagore bo mu Ijuru b’igikundiro, b’amaso manini)
52|21|Naho ba bandi bemeye maze ababakomokaho bakabakurikira mu kwemera, tuzabahuza n’ababakomotseho (mu ijuru), kandi nta cyo tuzigera tugabanya mu bikorwa byabo. Buri muntu azabazwa ibyo yakoze
52|22|Tuzabaha imbuto n’inyama (by’amoko yose) bazajya bifuza
52|23|Bazajya bahererekanyamo ibirahure by’ikinyobwa kitazabatera kuvuga amagambo adafite akamaro cyangwa ngo kibatere gukora ibyaha
52|24|Bazaba bazengurukwamo n’abahungu b’abahereza babo, bameze nk’inigi zishashagirana (Lu’ulu’u) zikiri mu bubiko bwazo
52|25|Bamwe muri bo bazajya bahindukira barebe bagenzi babo, babazanya
52|26|Bavuga bati “Mbere (ku isi) twabaga turi mu miryango yacu dufite ubwoba n’impungenge (z’ibihano bya Allah)”
52|27|“None Allah yatugororeye, aturinda ibihano by’umuriro utwika.”
52|28|Mu by’ukuri mbere twajyaga tumusenga (wenyine). Rwose ni We Mugiraneza, Nyirimbabazi
52|29|Bityo, (yewe Muhamadi) komeza wibutse! Mu by’ukuri ku bw’ingabire za Nyagasani wawe (zo kuba warahawe ubutumwa), ntabwo uri umupfumu cyangwa umusazi (nk’uko babivuga)
52|30|Ahubwo (abahakanyi) baravuga bati “(Muhamadi) ni umusizi, reka tumutege iminsi (azapfe nk’uko abandi basizi bapfuye)!”
52|31|Babwire uti “Ngaho nimutegereze, mu by’ukuri ndi kumwe namwe mu bategereje.”
52|32|Cyangwa imitekerereze yabo ni yo ibategeka (kuvuga) ibyo? Cyangwa ahubwo ni abantu barengera (imbibi za Allah)
52|33|Ndetse bavuga ko (Qur’an) yayihimbiye? (Oya), ahubwo ntibemera
52|34|Ngaho nibazane inkuru zimeze nk’iziyivugwamo (Qur’an), niba koko ari abanyakuri
52|35|Ese (bibwira ko) baremwe nta cyo bakomowemo, cyangwa ni bo baremyi
52|36|Cyangwa bibwira ko baremye ibirere n’isi? Ahubwo ntibizera
52|37|Cyangwa bibwira ko bafite ibigega bya Nyagasani wawe? Cyangwa ni bo bagenga (b’isi, bakora ibyo bashaka)
52|38|Cyangwa bibwira ko bafite urwego buririraho (bajya mu ijuru) ngo bumvirize ibivugirwayo? Ngaho umwumviriza wabo nazane ibimenyetso simusiga
52|39|Cyangwa bibwira ko (Allah) afite abakobwa, mwe mukagira abahungu
52|40|Cyangwa bibwira ko (wowe Muhamadi) ubasaba igihembo, none bakaba baremererwa n’ubwishyu
52|41|Cyangwa bibwira ko bazi ibyihishe, bakaba babyandika (badakeneye ibyo ubabwira)
52|42|Cyangwa icyo bashaka ni ubugambanyi? Nyamara abahakanye ni bo bazahanirwa ubugambanyi bwabo
52|43|Cyangwa bafite indi mana itari Allah? Ubutagatifu ni ubwa Allah kandi nta ho ahuriye n’ibyo bamubangikanya na byo
52|44|N’iyo baza kubona igice cy’ikirere kigwa hasi, bari kuvuga bati “Ni igicu gicucitse!”
52|45|Bareke kugeza ubwo bazahura n’umunsi wabo, aho bazagwa igihumure bagapfa (kubera ibihano)
52|46|Umunsi imigambi mibisha yabo itazagira icyo ibamarira, ndetse nta n’ubwo bazatabarwa
52|47|Kandi mu by’ukuri abakora ibibi bazahanishwa ibindi bihano (ku isi) mbere y’ibyo (ku munsi w’imperuka); ariko abenshi muri bo ntibabizi
52|48|Bityo (yewe Muhamadi), ihanganire itegeko rya Nyagasani wawe, kuko mu by’ukuri tuguhanzeho amaso. Ndetse unasingize ikuzo rya Nyagasani wawe igihe ubyutse (ugiye gusali)
52|49|No mu ijoro ujye umusingiza, ndetse n’igihe urumuri rw’inyenyeri ruba rugenda rukendera
53|1|Ndahiye inyenyeri igihe irenga
53|2|(Ko uyu) mugenzi wanyu (Intumwa Muhamadi) atigeze ayoba ndetse ko atigeze anateshuka (ku nzira y’ukuri)
53|3|Nta n’ubwo avuga ashingiye ku marangamutima ye
53|4|Ahubwo (ibyo avuga) ni ibyo ahishurirwa (na Allah)
53|5|Yigishijwe (iyi Qur’an) n’umunyembaraga cyane (Malayika Jibrilu)
53|6|Ufite ububasha kandi utagira inenge, wagaragariye (Intumwa Muhamadi) mu ishusho ye y’ukuri
53|7|Ubwo (Malayika Jibrilu) yari mu kirere cyo hejuru
53|8|Nuko yegera (Intumwa Muhamadi), maze aramanuka akomeza kuyegera
53|9|(Yamwegereye) mu ntera ingana n’iri hagati y’amahembe abiri y’umuheto cyangwa bugufi kurushaho
53|10|Nuko (Allah) ahishurira umugaragu we (Muhamadi, abinyujije kuri Malayika Jibrilu) ibyo yagombaga kumuhishurira byose
53|11|Umutima (wa Muhamadi) ntiwigeze ubeshya ku byo wabonye
53|12|None se muramugisha impaka ku byo yabonye (ubwo yazamukaga mu ijuru rya karindwi)
53|13|Kandi rwose (Muhamadi) yaramubonye (Malayika Jibrilu) ubwo yamanukaga ku yindi nshuro
53|14|Ubwo yari kuri Sidrat-il-Muntaha (Igiti cya nyuma)
53|15|Ni na ho hari ubuturo bw’ijuru (ry’abemeramana)
53|16|Ubwo icyo giti (Sidrat) cyatwikirwaga n’ibyagitwikiriye (urumuri rutangaje)
53|17|Indoro (y’Intumwa y’Imana) ntiyigeze itana, cyangwa ngo irengere (imbibi yari yashyiriweho)
53|18|Mu by’ukuri (Intumwa Muhamadi) yabonye bimwe mu bitangaza bihambaye bya Nyagasani wayo
53|19|Ese ntimutekereza (ku bigirwamana musenga); Laata na Uza
53|20|Ndetse na Manaata, ikindi (kigirwamana) cya gatatu
53|21|Ese mwibwira ko mufite abana b’abahungu naho We (Allah) akagira ab’abakobwa
53|22|Iryo ryaba ari igabana ribogamye
53|23|Ibyo (bigirwamana) nta kindi biri cyo usibye kuba ari amazina masa mwabihimbiye, mwe n’abakurambere banyu, Allah atigeze abahera uburenganzira. Rwose nta kindi bakurikira kitari ugukekeranya ndetse n’ibyo imitima (yabo) irarikira. Kandi mu by’ukuri bagezweho n’umuyoboro uturutse kwa Nyagasani wabo
53|24|Ese (mutekereza ko) umuntu yabona ibyo yifuza byose
53|25|Allah ni We Mugenga w’ubuzima bw’imperuka n’ubw’isi
53|26|None se ni bangahe mu bamalayika bari mu birere, ubuvugizi bwabo butazigera bugira icyo bumara Allah atabanje kubitangira uburenganzira bikagirira akamaro uwo ashatse kandi yishimira
53|27|Mu by’ukuri abatemera imperuka bita abamalayika amazina y’igitsina gore
53|28|Kandi ibyo nta bumenyi babifitiye. Ndetse nta kindi bakurikira kitari ugukekeranya, kandi rwose ugukeka nta cyo kuvuze imbere y’ukuri
53|29|Bityo, irengagize wa wundi wateye umugongo urwibutso rwacu nta kindi ashaka uretse ubuzima bw’isi
53|30|(Ibyo bavuga) ni ho ubumenyi bwabo bugarukira. Mu by’ukuri Nyagasani wawe ni We uzi neza uwayobye inzira ye, kandi ni na We uzi neza abayobotse
53|31|Kandi ibiri mu birere n’ibiri mu isi ni ibya Allah, (yashyizeho ayo mategeko) kugira ngo ahane inkozi z’ibibi kubera ibyo zakoze, ndetse anahembe ibyiza (ijuru) abakora ibyiza
53|32|Ba bandi birinda ibyaha bikomeye n’ibikozasoni uretse kuba bagwa mu byaha byoroshye; mu by’ukuri imbabazi za Nyagasani wawe ziragutse. Ni We ubazi neza kuva yabarema abakuye mu gitaka, n’igihe mwari insoro muri nyababyeyi za ba nyoko. Bityo, ntimukigire abere kuko ari We uzi neza umugandukira
53|33|Ese (yewe Muhamadi) wabonye wa wundi wateye umugongo (akanga kumvira Allah)
53|34|Akanatanga bike (mu byo twamuhaye), nyuma akabireka burundu
53|35|Ese yaba afite ubumenyi bw’ibitagaragara akaba abona (ko ibyo intumwa Muhamadi yahishuriwe atari ukuri)
53|36|Cyangwa ntiyabwiwe ibiri mu bitabo bya Musa
53|37|Ndetse n’ibiri mu bya Ibrahimu wasohoje ubutumwa
53|38|Ko nta we uzikorera umutwaro w’undi
53|39|Kandi ko nta cyo umuntu azabona (ku munsi w’imperuka) usibye ibyo yashyizemo umuhate
53|40|Kandi ko umuhate we uzagaragara (ku munsi w’imperuka)
53|41|Maze akazabihemberwa ibihembo byuzuye
53|42|Kandi ko iherezo (rya buri kintu) ari kwa Nyagasani wawe
53|43|Kandi ko ari We (Allah) utera guseka (kwishima) no kurira (kubabara)
53|44|No kuba ari We wisubiza ubuzima ndetse akanabutanga
53|45|No kuba ari we waremye ibitsina byombi, gabo na gore
53|46|Mu ntanga igihe zisohowe

53|51|N’aba Thamudu ntiyagira uwo asigaza
53|52|Na mbere yabo, (yoretse) abantu ba Nuhu. Mu by’ukuri bari inkozi z’ibibi bakaba n’abarengera (amategeko ya Allah) bikabije
53|53|Ndetse n’imidugudu (ya Sodoma) yabirinduwe, ni We wayibirinduye (ibyari hasi bijya hejuru n’ibyari hejuru bijya hasi)
53|54|Nuko (iyo midugudu) itwikirwa n’ibyayitwikiriye (ibihano bigizwe n’amabuye)
53|55|None se (yewe muntu) ni izihe nema za Nyagasani wawe ushidikanyaho (ko atari ize)
53|56|Uyu (Muhamadi) ni umwe mu (ruhererekane rw’) ababurizi bo hambere
53|57|Umunsi w’imperuka uregereje

53|59|None se mutangajwe n’aya magambo (ya Qur’an)
53|60|Mukaba museka (muyihakana) aho kurira
53|61|Muhugiye mu bibarangaza
53|62|Bityo, nimwubamire Allah munamugaragire (wenyine)
54|1|Igihe cy’imperuka kiregereje ndetse n’ukwezi kwarasadutse
54|2|N’iyo (abahakanyi) babonye igitangaza, batera umugongo bakavuga bati “Ubu ni uburozi bugikomeje!”
54|3|Barahakanye banakurikira irari ryabo, kandi buri kintu kizagira iherezo
54|4|Kandi rwose bagezweho n’inkuru zibabuza (gukora ibibi)
54|5|(Izo nkuru ziri muri Qur’an) zuje ubushishozi buhebuje, ariko uko kubaburira nta cyo kwabamariye
54|6|Bityo (yewe Muhamadi), birengagize kandi (unabibutse) umunsi umuhamagazi azahamagarira kugana ku kintu kibi cyane (gucirwa urubanza ku munsi w’imperuka)
54|7|Bazaba bubitse amaso (kubera ikimwaro), basohoka mu mva bameze nk’inzige zinyanyagiye
54|8|Bihuta bagana uhamagara. Abahakanyi bazavuga bati “Uyu ni umunsi ugoye.”
54|9|Na mbere yabo, abantu ba Nuhu bahinyuye umugaragu wacu, maze baravuga bati “Ni umusazi”, ndetse aranamaganwa
54|10|Nuko asaba Nyagasani we (agira ati) “Rwose njye naneshejwe, ngaho tabara!”
54|11|Nuko dufungura amarembo y’ikirere, hamanuka amazi yisuka ari menshi
54|12|Nuko isi tuyikuramo amasoko, maze amazi (yo mu nsi no hejuru) arahura ku bw’itegeko ryagenwe
54|13|Maze (Nuhu) tumutwara mu gikozwe mu mbaho n’imisumari (inkuge)
54|14|Cyagendaga (hejuru y’amazi) tugihanze amaso; (ibyo) biba igihembo cy’uwo bahakanye
54|15|Rwose (iyi nkuru ya Nuhu) twarayiretse ngo ibe ikimenyetso (n’isomo ku bazaza nyuma ye). Ese hari uwibuka (ngo bimugirire akamaro)
54|16|Mbega uko ibihano byanjye no kuburira kwanjye byari bimeze
54|17|Kandi rwose Qur’an twarayoroheje kugira ngo ibe urwibutso. Ese hari uwibuka (ngo bimugirire akamaro)
54|18|Aba Adi bahinyuye (Intumwa yabo Hudu); mbega uko ibihano byanjye no kuburira kwanjye byari bimeze
54|19|Mu by’ukuri twaboherereje inkubi y’umuyaga uvuza ubuhuha ku munsi w’amakuba akomeye
54|20|Uterura abantu bakamera nk’ingiga z’ibiti by’imitende byaranduwe
54|21|Mbega uko ibihano byanjye no kuburira kwanjye byari bimeze
54|22|Kandi rwose Qur’an twarayoroheje kugira ngo ibe urwibutso. Ese hari uwibuka (ngo bimugirire akamaro)
54|23|Aba Thamudi bahinyuye kuburira (kwacu)
54|24|Nuko baravuga bati “Ese ni gute twafata umuntu umwe unadukomokamo ngo tube ari we dukurikira? Rwose ubwo twaba turi mu buyobe n’ubusazi!”
54|25|Ese ubu koko urwibutso ni we wenyine muri twe rwahawe? Ahubwo we ni umubeshyi akaba n’umwibone
54|26|Bidatinze bazamenya umubeshyi w’umwibone uwo ari we
54|27|Tugiye kuboherereza ingamiya (y’ingore) kugira ngo tubagerageze; bityo bagenzure unabihanganire
54|28|Unababwire ko amazi bagomba kuyasangira na yo (ingamiya); buri wese azajya agira igihe cye cyo kuyanywaho
54|29|Ariko bahamagaye mugenzi wabo (afata inkota) arayica
54|30|Mbega uko ibihano byanjye no kuburira kwanjye byari bimeze
54|31|Mu by’ukuri twaboherereje urusaku rumwe gusa, maze bamera nk’ibyatsi byumye byaribaswe
54|32|Kandi rwose Qur’an twarayoroheje kugira ngo ibe urwibutso. Ese hari uwibuka (ngo bimugirire akamaro)
54|33|Abantu ba Lutwi bahinyuye kuburira (kwacu)
54|34|Twaboherereje inkubi y’umuyaga uvanze n’amabuye (ubarimbura bose), usibye gusa umuryango wa Lutwi twarokoye mu rukerera
54|35|(Ibyo twabikoze) ku bw’ingabire ziduturutseho. Uko ni ko duhemba ushimira
54|36|Nyamara (Lutwi) yari yarababuriye ko bazahura n’ibihano byacu, nuko bashidikanya kuri uko kuburira (kwacu)
54|37|Baranamwinginze (ngo abahe) abashyitsi be (kugira ngo babakorere ubutinganyi). Nuko tubahuma amaso (tuvuga tuti) “Ngaho nimusogongere ibihano byanjye no kuburira (kwanjye)!”
54|38|Kandi rwose twabazindukirije mu bihano bikomeza (kuzageza ku munsi w’imperuka)
54|39|Ngaho nimusogongere ibihano byanjye no ku byo najyaga mbaburira
54|40|Kandi rwose Qur’an twarayoroheje kugira ngo ibe urwibutso. Ese hari uwibuka (ngo bimugirire akamaro)
54|41|Kandi rwose kuburira (kwanjye) kwageze ku bantu ba Farawo
54|42|Bahinyuye ibitangaza byacu byose, nuko turabafata tubahanisha ibihano by’Umunyacyubahiro bihebuje, Ushobora byose
54|43|Ese abahakanyi banyu (b’i Maka) ni bo beza kurusha abo (abantu ba Adi, aba Thamudi, aba Nuhu n’aba Farawo, boretswe)? Cyangwa mufite ubudahangarwa bwanditse mu bitabo (bwo kutazahanwa)
54|44|Cyangwa (abo bahakanyi) baravuga bati “Twe turi benshi dushyize hamwe, dushoboye kwitabara!”
54|45|Nyamara abo bishyize hamwe bazatsindwa banayabangire ingata
54|46|Ahubwo umunsi w’imperuka ni cyo gihe basezeranyijwe (cyo kuzahanirwaho), ndetse imperuka izaba iteye ubwoba cyane kandi irura
54|47|Mu by’ ukuri, inkozi z’ibibi ziri mu buyobe (hano ku isi) kandi zizahanishwa umuriro utwika
54|48|Umunsi uburanga bwabo buzakururirwa mu muriro (bazabwirwa bati) “Ngaho nimwumve igihano cy’umuriro.”
54|49|Mu by’ukuri buri kintu twakiremye ku rugero twagennye (igeno ryacyo)
